I didn‚Äôt feel confused but was surprised that it was excellent. As soon as you enter the lobby, you will see a potted plant that looks like a sky rocket. Although the front desk does not look big, the front desk told us that they will check in one room at a time. They also have their own small potted plant on the front desk table, which looks OK. The day before check-in, the housekeeper will call and add WeChat to inform you of the route and ask if you need to order food, etc. 40 minutes after driving through the south gate of Chengdu, we saw a pastoral scenery that we liked. The hotel building is also in the style of Western Sichuan folk houses, harmoniously coexisting with the village and not out of place. It was 11:30 in the morning, and we had not yet come out of the room, so we went to pick vegetables in the hotel‚Äôs vegetable patch. This was also the children‚Äôs favorite part of this trip. Although the radishes have almost been pulled out, the pea tips have been recuperating for a week after New Year's Day and are fresh and tender, just in time for picking. After picking it, the restaurant cleaned it and boiled it directly into the local chicken soup. It was delicious. Children from households that have difficulty eating vegetables also eat a lot of the fruits of their own labor.
After lunch, we came out of the room. The floor heating was very comfortable and the hot spring pool was right at the door (remember not to close the door when taking a bath, let alone lock the room key in the room. Don't ask us how we knew this). I was given a set of children‚Äôs toiletries from Mustela. The quality of the welcome fruits is also pretty good.

We also had a small hot pot dinner at the hotel. The portions were sufficient. We didn‚Äôt finish the set meal for two. The food was fresh, but the spicy hotpot taste was just mediocre in Chengdu.
The next day, I made an appoin**ent with a photographer to take a New Year's family portrait at the hotel. After communicating with the housekeeper, I arranged a guest room to help me briefly tidy up the room. The service response was very timely.
In addition to the complimentary picking in the room, we also got complimentary picking during our lunch and evening meals, which was a real treat for children who like picking in the fields.
All in all, it was a relaxing and enjoyable micro-vacation in the surrounding area, worth recommending.
If I have to say something negative, it is that the floor heating is very warm, the quilt is a little thick, and it is a bit hot to sleep on.

posted:Posted January 2, 2024
msg:Perhaps I have always thought that Anlu is the sister brand of Aman, so with such a high price, I naturally have high expectations. The design of the hotel is very good, but other aspects are really hard to describe.

In terms of hygiene, there was a bathroom smell in the shower room. I called the staff, but they said they couldn't smell it at first. Strongly request to change room. Later I changed rooms.

While eating dinner, I sent a message to the housekeeper to put the water in the outdoor pool for soaking. The housekeeper replied that it would only take less than 15 minutes to fill up the water. Then we thought about putting water in the hot spring and soaking in it before going to bed later.

The restaurant's dinner offerings were even more shocking. It felt like a farmhouse, but some of the dishes tasted really bad. The only thing I think is that the fried vegetables are okay. Even the other tomato scrambled eggs had a fishy smell. Of course don't expect breakfast. It didn't feel like a 5-star hotel at all. There was no buffet breakfast and I lost my appetite when I saw some. The taste is mediocre.

When I got to the room in the evening, I asked the housekeeper to put the water in. I was told that it would take 30-45 minutes to put the water in. After waiting for a long time, when it was half full, I went to soak my feet. The water was found to be almost lukewarm. Hey, give up

By the way, there is a charge for tea bags in the room, which is 28 yuan per bag. There is also a charge for large bottles of mineral water. Please pay attention.

All in all, this is the worst hotel I have ever stayed in. After some research, it turns out that the Anlu Hotel series is a domestic brand. It has nothing to do with the Aman Group.

The surrounding area of the hotel still needs to be developed, and there are not many places to play around. If you have travel purposes, it is best to drive by yourself and then go around.
The hardware of the hotel is still relatively limited as a whole. There are few types of breakfast, some items of the dinner are missing, and the surrounding desolation interacts with the hotel's own amu*****t facilities, which leads to fewer options, which is relatively the same as the price of Six Senses Song Pin. It will be interesting (also related to the actual site selection).
However, I always feel that these resort hotels in Chengdu are almost meaningless in all aspects...
